#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_academic_session
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_academic_session` (
  `aca_session_id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `session` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `startDate` date NOT NULL,
  `endDate` date NOT NULL,
  `studyMode` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`aca_session_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=3 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_academic_session (`aca_session_id`, `session`, `startDate`, `endDate`, `studyMode`, `deleted`, `status`) VALUES (1, 14, '2013-02-28', '2013-11-30', 1, 0, 1);

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_activities
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_activities` (
  `activity_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `activity` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `module` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(12) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`activity_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=277 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_countries
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_countries` (
  `iso` char(2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'US',
  `name` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `printable_name` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `iso3` char(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `numcode` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`iso`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_course_registration
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_course_registration` (
  `courseReg_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `progSubject_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `semester_session_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  `modified_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`courseReg_id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `progSubject_id` (`progSubject_id`,`semester_session_id`),
  KEY `semester_session_id` (`semester_session_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_email_queue
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_email_queue` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `to_email` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `subject` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `alt_message` text,
  `max_attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '3',
  `attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `success` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `date_published` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_attempt` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_sent` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_login_attempts
#

  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ip_address` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `login` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `time` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_prog_semester_unit
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_prog_semester_unit` (
  `progSU_id` int(6) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `prog_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `minimumUnit` int(3) NOT NULL,
  `maximumUnit` int(3) NOT NULL,
  `progLevel` int(6) NOT NULL,
  `progSemester` int(6) NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`progSU_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=3 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `prog_id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `course_id` int(10) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=50 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_roles
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_roles` (
  `role_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `role_name` varchar(60) NOT NULL,
  `description` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `default` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `can_delete` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `login_destination` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '/',
  `deleted` int(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `default_context` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'content',
  PRIMARY KEY (`role_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_user_cookies
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_user_cookies` (
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  KEY `token` (`token`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_user_meta
#

  `meta_id` int(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  `meta_value` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`meta_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=40 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_users
#

CREATE TABLE `bf_users` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `role_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '4',
  `email` varchar(120) NOT NULL DEFAULT '''username''@bondev.dev',
  `username` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `password_hash` char(60) NOT NULL,
  `reset_hash` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `firstname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `middlename` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `lastname` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `last_login` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `last_ip` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `reset_by` int(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `banned` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ban_message` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `display_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `display_name_changed` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `timezone` char(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'UM6',
  `language` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'english',
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `activate_hash` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `password_iterations` int(4) NOT NULL,
  `force_password_reset` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=25 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
